/* Business values we test against are defined as regexes:
 * - mobile tests
 * - preference cookie key/value pairs
 * - no_mobile query_string key/value pair
 *
 * The remainder are defined as strings
 * - referrer cookie
 * - mobile path
 */
    var version = 1.2,
        pref_mob = /TI_PREFS=phone/,
        pref_tab = /TI_PREFS=tablet/,
        pref_def = /TI_PREFS=default/,
        no_mob   = /nomobile=1/,
        omniture_cookie = 'orig_ref',
        mob_path = '/m',
        cookie = document.cookie,
        redirect = function() {
        /* Build mobile version of the url */
            var mob_url  = location.href.replace(site_root, function(match, idx, url){
                // Check if redirect to site_root, and if so, append a trailing
                // slash to avoid a server-side redirect (301) on bare url.
                  var is_root = match.length + idx === url.length;
                  return match + mob_path + (is_root ? '/' : '');
                });

        /* Set preference for mobile */
            document.cookie = pref_mob.source;

        /* Set Omniture cookie to capture referrer */
            document.cookie = omniture_cookie + '=' + document.referrer + '; path=/';
        /* Execute redirect */
     	    location.href = mob_url;
     };

/* If preference for default or tablet, skip redirect */
    if (pref_def.test(cookie) || pref_tab.test(cookie)) {
        return;
    }

/* Honor no_mobile request by updating cookie and skipping redirect */
    if (no_mob.test(location.search)) {
        document.cookie = pref_def.source;
        return;
    }

/* Redirect if pref_mobile cookie or if a user_agent target,
 * otherwise indicate prefernce for default version
 */
    if (pref_mob.test(cookie)) {
        redirect();
    } else {
        document.cookie = pref_def.source;
    }

          <h1 id="content-title">
           How to Do the Perfect Squat
          </h1>
          <!--div class="blog"-->
          <h2 class="dek">
           By
           <a href="http://dailyburn.com/?partner=life_health&amp;mtype=5&amp;sub_id=06232014_squatvideo&amp;utm_source=life_health&amp;utm_medium=life_health&amp;utm_campaign=06232014_squatvideo&amp;utm_content=06232014_06232014_squatvideo" target="_blank">
            DailyBurn
           </a>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The squat is one of the best moves to tone your glutes and trim your thighs, but it's important to be sure your form is correct to maximize results and prevent injuries.
           <a href="http://dailyburn.com/?partner=life_health&amp;mtype=5&amp;sub_id=06232014_squatvideo&amp;utm_source=life_health&amp;utm_medium=life_health&amp;utm_campaign=06232014_squatvideo&amp;utm_content=06232014_06232014_squatvideo" target="_blank">
            DailyBurn
           </a>
           trainer Anja Garcia shows you how.
          </h2>
          <span class="vtags">
           #legs&amp;butt #strength
          </span>
         </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   tp = tp || {};
	tp.aid = "RZb7RBAyqB";
	tp.tisub = function() {
	var _isUserValid = function() {
		return tp.util.findCookieByName("TISub") ? true : false;
	};
	var _hasAccessToAppAid = function(appId) {
		if (_isUserValid()) {
			var TISubCookieData = _deserializeTISub(tp.util.findCookieByName("TISub"));
			if(TISubCookieData.availableAppIds &amp;&amp; TISubCookieData.availableAppIds.indexOf(appId) + 1) {
				return true;
			}
		}
		return false;
	};
	var _deserializeTISub = function(strCookie) {
		var cookie = decodeURIComponent(strCookie);
		var tempDataArr = cookie.split("|");
		var dataObj = {};
		for(var i = tempDataArr.length; i--;) {
			tempDataArr[i] = tempDataArr[i].split("~");
			dataObj[tempDataArr[i][0]] = tempDataArr[i][1];
		}
		return dataObj;
	};
	return {
		isUserValid : function() {
			return _isUserValid();
		},
		hasAccessToAppId : function(appId) {
			return _hasAccessToAppAid(appId);
		}
	};
}();

    tp.contentCreated = "";
	tp.contentAuthor = "";
	tp.contentSection = "";
	tp.init(function() {
	userHasAccess = tp.tisub.hasAccessToAppId('health.com.paywall');
shouldTrack = !userHasAccess;
tp.meter.init({
	paywallID: '77086773',
	trackPageview: false,
	meterSelector: function () {     
		if(tp.tisub.isUserValid())             
			return "SubsMeter";
		else
			return "RegMeter";
	},
	onMeterInactive: function (meter) {
		userHasAccess = true;
		shouldTrack = false;
		trackPageview = false;
	},
	onMeterActive: function (meter) { 
		document.cookie = 'TICM_pcs_meter=' + (meter.views &gt; meter.max_views ? meter.max_views : meter.views).toString() + '; path=/; domain=.health.com;';
	},
	onMeterExpired: function (meter) {
		document.cookie = 'TICM_pcs_meter=' + (meter.views &gt; meter.max_views ? meter.max_views : meter.views).toString() + '; path=/; domain=.health.com;';
	},
	onShowOffer: function () {
		return false;
	}
});
	});
